  <script>
   $sfr('.home').component({

    /**
     * Bind nodes
     */
    nodes: function () {
        this.$seoTexts = this.$element.find('.stack-seo__block');
        this.$seoMore = this.$element.find('.stack-seo__link');

        this.$wave1 = this.$element.find('.stack-intro .stack-wave__wave-container');
        this.$wave2 = this.$element.find('.stack-straight .stack-wave__wave-container');
        this.$wave3 = this.$element.find('.stack-left-right-left .stack-wave__wave-container');
        this.$wave4 = this.$element.find('.stack-left-right .stack-wave__wave-container');
    },

    /**
     * Bind events
     */
    events: function () {
        // On click on link to see more in seo stack
        this.$seoMore.click(this.moreSeo.bind(this));
    },

    /**
     * Initialize
     */
    init: function () {
        // New scrollmagic controller
        this.controller = new ScrollMagic.Controller();


        this.$wave1.data('width', this.$wave1.width()).data('height', this.$wave1.height()).data('percentage', 0);
        this.$wave2.data('width', this.$wave2.width()).data('height', this.$wave2.height()).data('percentage', 0);
        this.$wave3.data('width', this.$wave3.width()).data('height', this.$wave3.height()).data('percentage', 0);
        this.$wave4.data('width', this.$wave4.width()).data('height', this.$wave4.height()).data('percentage', 0);

        TweenMax.set(this.$wave1, {width : 0});
        TweenMax.set([this.$wave2, this.$wave3, this.$wave4], {height : 0});
        TweenMax.set([this.$wave1, this.$wave2, this.$wave3, this.$wave4], {display : 'block'});

        // If we are on mobile
        if (this.isMobile()) {
            // For each seo text
            this.$seoTexts.each(function (index, element) {
                // if not first
                if (index > 0) {
                    // Hide it
                    $sfr(element).hide();
                }
                // if first
                else {
                    // Shrink it
                    $sfr(element).css('height', '83px');
                }
            });
        // if not mobile
        } else {
            // Hide the link
            this.$seoMore.hide();
        }

        this.initTweenScene(this.$wave1, '#stack-intro', 1.5);
        this.initScrollScene(this.$wave2, '#stack-straight');
        this.initScrollScene(this.$wave3, '#stack-left-right-left');
        this.initScrollScene(this.$wave4, '#stack-left-right');

        // Init the lottie animation
        this.initLottieAnimation();
    },

    /**
     * Init of a scene stack wave
     * @param pElement
     * @param pSprite
     * @param pTrigger
     * @param pDelay
     */
    initTweenScene: function (pElement, pTrigger, pDelay) {

        // Create the tween
        var tween = TweenMax.to(pElement, 1.2, {
            height : pElement.data('height'),
            width : pElement.data('width'),
            delay: pDelay
        });

        // Create the scene
        var scene = new ScrollMagic.Scene({
            triggerElement: pTrigger,
            triggerHook: "onEnter"
        })
        .reverse(true)
        .setTween(tween)
        .addTo(this.controller);
    },

    initScrollScene : function(pElement, pTrigger){
        // Create the scene
        var scene = new ScrollMagic.Scene({
            triggerElement: pTrigger,
            triggerHook: "onLeave"
        })
            .on('update', function(pEvent){
                var windowBottom = $sfr(window).scrollTop() + $sfr(window).height();
                var elementTop = $sfr(pTrigger).offset().top + $sfr(pTrigger).height()/2;
                var percentage = (windowBottom - elementTop) / $sfr(pTrigger).height() * 100;
                
                if (windowBottom >= elementTop && percentage > pElement.data('percentage')) {
                    TweenMax.set(pElement, {
                        height : percentage+'%',
                    });

                    pElement.data('percentage', percentage);
                }
            })
            // .reverse(true)
            .addTo(this.controller);
    },


    /**
     * Init the bodymovin animation for stack family
     */
    initLottieAnimation: function () {
        var animation = lottie.loadAnimation({
            container: document.querySelector(".home-stack__animation"),
            renderer: 'svg',
            loop: true,
            autoplay: true,
            prerender: true,
            animationData: animationData,
            rendererSettings: {
                progressiveLoad: true, // Boolean, only svg renderer, loads dom elements when needed. Might speed up initialization for large number of elements.
                hideOnTransparent: true //Boolean, only svg renderer, hides elements when opacity reaches 0 (defaults to true)
            }
        });
    },

    /**
     * Event on seo link click
     * @param pEvent
     */
    moreSeo: function (pEvent) {
        pEvent.preventDefault();

        // Show all the seo texts
        this.$seoTexts.show().css('height', 'auto');

        // Hide the link
        $sfr(pEvent.target).hide();
    },

    /**
     * Return if we are on mobile or not
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    isMobile: function () {
        return window.matchMedia("(max-width: 767px)").matches;
    }

});
  </script>
  <script charset="UTF-8" src="//static.s-sfr.fr/stats/footer.js">
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
